The main tools of the printer are wooden blocks in different shapes - square , rectangle , oval , round and semi @-@ circular or crescent - and sizes called bunta . Blocks are hand @-@ carved of seasoned teak wood by trained craftsmen . The blocks for imprinting are hand @-@ carved by skilled artisans in wood . These hand @-@ carved block are used to imprint the design onto the fabric . The imprinting is done by hand by a skilled block printer . Taavi Women Black &amp; Maroon Solid Block Print Legacy Longline Top with Flared Sleeves Special Technique / Craft : Block printing is a manual technique of using hand @-@ carved wooden blocks to create impressions on a cloth . The main tools of the printer are wooden blocks in different shapes - square , rectangle , oval , round and crescent - in a measuring scale called bunta . Blocks are carved mainly of seasoned teak wood by trained craftsmen . Motifs which are still prominent are mostly floral , vegetal and animal figures such as elephants and peacocks . Taavi Women Coffee Brown &amp; Green Kalamkari Hand Block Print A @-@ Line Skirt with Slit Special Technique / Craft : Kalamkari is a type of hand @-@ painted or block @-@ printed cotton textile , wherein motifs are inspired from the folklore and are hand painted using the tool of kalam directly onto the fabric . The process involves washing , rinsing , soaking and bleaching the fabric and applying mordants and dyes using natural substances like indigo ( blue ) , madder ( red ) , mango bark ( yellow ) and palm sugar ( black ) . Painting on the fabric is done with a kalam , charcoal and myrobalan paste . Taavi Women Black &amp; Off @-@ White Checked Inspired By Craft Print Legacy Asymmetric Top Special Technique / Craft : Block printing is a manual technique of using hand @-@ carved &amp; nbsp ; wooden blocks to create impressions on a cloth . The main tools of the printer are wooden blocks in different shapes - square , rectangle , oval , round and crescent - in a measuring scale called bunta . Blocks are carved mainly of seasoned teak wood by trained craftsmen . Taavi Women Grey &amp; Black Hand Block Print Legacy A @-@ Line Dress with Contrast Flounce Hem Special Technique / Craft : Block printing is a process of using wooden blocks to create impressions on a cloth . The main tools of the printer are wooden blocks in different shapes - square , rectangle , oval , round and semi @-@ circular or crescent - and sizes called bunta . Blocks are hand @-@ carved of seasoned teak wood by trained craftsmen . The blocks for imprinting are hand @-@ carved by skilled artisans in wood . These hand @-@ carved blocks are used to imprint the design onto the fabric . The imprinting is done by hand by a skilled block printer . Taavi Men Red &amp; Beige Kalamkari Block Printed Regular Fit Shirt with Roll @-@ Up Sleeves Special Technique / Craft : Kalamkari is a type of hand @-@ painted or block @-@ printed cotton textile , wherein motifs are inspired by the folklore and are hand @-@ painted using the tool of kalam directly onto the fabric . The process involves washing , rinsing , soaking and bleaching the fabric and applying mordants and dyes using natural substances like indigo ( blue ) , madder ( red ) , mango bark ( yellow ) and palm sugar ( black ) . Painting on the fabric is done with a kalam , charcoal and myrobalan paste . Taavi Women Blue Block Print Legacy A @-@ Line Maxi Flared Skirt Special Technique / Craft : Block printing is a process of using wodden blocks to create impressions on a cloth . The main tools of the printer are wooden blocks in different shapes - square , rectangle , oval , round and semi @-@ circular or crescent - and sizes called bunta . Blocks are hand @-@ carved of seasoned teak wood by trained craftsmen . The blocks for imprinting are hand @-@ carved by skilled artisans in wood . These hand @-@ carved block are used to imprint the design onto the fabric . The imprinting is done by hand by a skilled block printer . Taavi Women Beige &amp; Blue Kalamkari Hand Block Print Top with Pockets Special Technique / Craft : Kalamkari is a type of hand @-@ painted or block @-@ printed cotton textile , wherein motifs are inspired from the folklore and are hand painted using the tool of kalam directly onto the fabric . The process involves washing , rinsing , soaking and bleaching the fabric and applying mordants and dyes using natural substances like indigo ( blue ) , madder ( red ) , mango bark ( yellow ) and palm sugar ( black ) . Painting on the fabric is done with a kalam , charcoal and myrobalan paste . Taavi Men Black Kalamkari Block Printed Regular Fit Casual Shirt with Roll @-@ Up Sleeves Special Technique / Craft : Kalamkari is a type of hand @-@ painted or block @-@ printed cotton textile , wherein motifs are inspired by the folklore and are hand @-@ painted using the tool of kalam directly onto the fabric . The process involves washing , rinsing , soaking and bleaching the fabric and applying mordants and dyes using natural substances like indigo ( blue ) , madder ( red ) , mango bark ( yellow ) and palm sugar ( black ) . Painting on the fabric is done with a kalam , charcoal and myrobalan paste . Taavi Women Orange Kantha Angrakha Kurta with Pockets &amp; Embroidered Detail Special Technique / Craft : A unique traditional art from Murshidabad , Kantha Work is embroidery work done on old sarees , dhotis and other apparel , is popular and is practised in Bengal , especially in Bholpur , and Bihar . It consists generally a running stitch on the sarees in the form of motifs such as animals , birds , flowers , simple geometrical shapes and scenes from everyday life . Taavi Women Multicoloured Checked Hand Block Print Legacy High @-@ Low Top with a Tie @-@ Up Neck Special Technique / Craft : Block printing is a process of using wooden blocks to create impressions on a cloth . The main tools of the printer are wooden blocks in different shapes - square , rectangle , oval , round and semi @-@ circular or crescent - and sizes called bunta . Blocks are hand @-@ carved of seasoned teak wood by trained craftsmen . The blocks for imprinting are hand @-@ carved by skilled artisans in wood . These hand @-@ carved blocks are used to imprint the design onto the fabric . The imprinting is done by hand by a skilled block printer . Taavi Women Grey Ajrakh Hand Block Print Straight Kurta with Button Closure Special Technique / Craft : Ajrakh : The authentic Ajrakh is printed on both sides by a method known as resist printing . This form of printing is done by hand with hand @-@ carved wooden blocks . Several different blocks are used to give the characteristic repeated patterning . Traditional &apos; Ajrakh &apos; involves various stages of dyeing and resist printing using natural dyes and mordants . Indigo and madder are the primary colours that are used for dyeing . The resist and some colours are printed on the cloth using carved wooden blocks . These blocks are carved with intricate symmetrical patterns so that the same block can be used for both sides of the clot Design : Region : Rajasthan and GujaratGreyStraight hand block printed kurtaRound neck with a small button placketThree @-@ quarter sleevesStraight hem with side slitsAjrakh Hand Block PrintDisclaimer : This is a handcrafted kurta , and is prone to colour bleeding due to use of natural dyesThe print on the garment might be unevenly owning to the handcrafted nature of the product , adding essence to the garment .

Taavi Women Black &amp; Yellow Block Print Legacy Palazzos with Pleats Special Technique / Craft : Block printing is a process of using wodden blocks to create impressions on a cloth .
